          <a href="/news/article-3161264/Escape-foot-roads-liquify-start-running-hear-dogs-barking-Geographers-offer-advice-survive-earthquake-predicted-obliterate-Pacific-Northwest.html">
           <img alt="The Cascadia Earthquake.

Cascadia_earthquake_sources.png  
Cascadia subduction zone
From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia

The area of the Cascadia subduction zone.
Coordinates: 45N 124W The Cascadia subduction zone (also referred to as the Cascadia fault) is a convergent plate boundary that stretches from northern Vancouver Island to northern California. It is a very long sloping subduction zone fault that separates the Juan de Fuca and North America plates.

The denser oceanic plate is subducting beneath the less dense continental plate offshore of British Columbia, Washington and Oregon. The North American Plate moves in a general southwest direction, overriding the oceanic plate. The Cascadia Subduction Zone is where the two plates meet.

Tectonic processes active in the Cascadia subduction zone region include accretion, subduction, deep earthquakes, and active volcanism that has included such notable eruptions as Mount Mazama (Crater Lake) about 7,500 years ago, Mount Meager a" height="115" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2015/07/14/19/2A874F1000000578-0-image-m-74_1436899600067.jpg" width="154"/>
           <span class="wocc bdrcc">
            Escape on foot because roads will liquefy and start running when you hear dogs barking: Geographers offer advice on how to survive the earthquake predicted to obliterate the Pacific Northwest
           </span>
          </a>
         </li>

       <div class="article-text wide" id="js-article-text">
        <h1>
         A reality show too far? New U.S. series films women giving BIRTH in the wild with no help from doctors
        </h1>
        <ul>
         <li>
          <font style="font-size:1.4em;">
           <span style="font-weight: bold;">
            Born in the Wild will follow young parents who take home birth to the next level by leaving even shelter behind
           </span>
          </font>
         </li>
         <li>
          <font style="font-size:1.4em;">
           <span style=" font-weight: bold;">
            The show was inspired by a viral YouTube video that's racked up 20M views and shows a woman giving birth in a tropical creek
           </span>
          </font>
         </li>
         <li>
          <font style="font-size:1.4em;">
           <span style="  font-weight: bold;">
            Producers say no first-time mothers will be allowed and that the TV crew's presence will increase safety for the mothers--but there will be no doctors
           </span>
          </font>
         </li>
         <li>
          <font style="font-size:1.4em;">
           <span style="   font-weight: bold;">
            Critics fear the show will start a dangerous trend that will endanger mother and child
           </span>
          </font>
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p class="author-section mol-para-with-font byline-plain">
         By
         <a class="author" href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Joshua+Gardner" rel="nofollow">
          Joshua Gardner
         </a>
        </p>
        <p class="byline-section mol-para-with-font">
         <span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-published">
          <span class="article-timestamp-label">
           Published:
          </span>
          01:10 EST, 5 June 2014
         </span>
         |
         <span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-updated">
          <span class="article-timestamp-label">
           Updated:
          </span>
          02:36 EST, 5 June 2014
         </span>
        </p>
        <div id="articleIconLinksContainer">
         <ul>
          <li class="share-facebook">

          <li class="share-twitter">

          <li class="share-pinterest">
          </li>
          <li class="share-gplus">

New Lifetime reality show to film women giving BIRTH in the wild with no help from doctors">
            <a>
            </a>

          <li class="share-email">
           <a class="js-email" data-ajax-refresh-everytime="true" data-modal-id="email-modal-overlay" data-modal-type="email-overlay" data-on-mobile="mailto:?subject=A step too far?            </a>
          </li>

         <a class="comments-count home" href="/news/article-2649274/A-step-far-New-Lifetime-reality-film-women-giving-BIRTH-wild-no-help-doctors.html#comments">
          <span>

        </div>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          A new reality show announced by Lifetime on Wednesday will follow young parents who forego not only hospitals during the birthing process, but also any shelter at all.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          Born in the Wild will portray the men and women who decide that giving birth surrounded by only the beauty and serenity of nature and away from any doctors or modern interventions is the way to go.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          Inspired by the huge popularity of a YouTube video that shows a woman giving birth in a tropical creek, some critics say such a show could kick off a dangerous trend that will endanger mothers and their babies alike.
         </font>
        </p>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
        <div class="artSplitter">
         <img alt="Born in the Wild: Lifetime has announced they'll air a show that follows parents who decide to give birth in nature with no doctors" class="blkBorder img-share" height="346" id="i-60b70197ad7adb4a" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2014/06/05/article-0-1E7B6EBB00000578-258_634x346.jpg" width="634"/>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Born in the Wild: Lifetime has announced they'll air a show that follows parents who decide to give birth in nature with no doctors
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          'What happens when the craziest experience of a womans life becomes truly wild, and soon-to-be parents decide to take on an unassisted birth in the outdoors?' wonders the press release.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          Producers hope the answer is ratings gold as Americans accustomed to hyper sterile hospital births and who are only starting to learn of the rising trend in home births watch with rapt attention.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
        </p>
        <div class="related-carousel with-fb news half" data-track-module="am-related_carousel^related_carousel" data-track-pos="static" data-track-selector=".rotator-panels a:not([class*=external])" id="p-16">
         <div class="rotator bdrcc">
          <div class="rotator-title">

        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          Lifetime says the show's subjects may not be first-time parents and will be closely watched by crews.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          'Were taking extreme precautions to make sure the mothers and the babies are safe,' Eli Lehrer, Lifetimes senior VP and head of nonfiction programming, told Entertainment Weekly. 'Our presence at these births is going to make them far safer than if they were doing it on their own.'
         </font>
        </p>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
        <div class="artSplitter">
         <div class="splitLeft">
          <img alt="Inspiring: The show was inspired by this woman's video, which showed her giving birth in a creek bed and has racked up 20 million views since February" class="blkBorder img-share" height="323" id="i-1069efc6a2a3030f" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2014/06/05/article-0-1E7B6EB700000578-382_306x323.jpg" width="306"/>
         </div>
         <div class="splitRight">
          <img alt="Inspiring: The show was inspired by this woman's video, which showed her giving birth in a creek bed and has racked up 20 million views since February" class="blkBorder img-share" height="323" id="i-623dfaf5a0232a4a" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2014/06/05/article-0-1E7B6EAB00000578-200_306x323.jpg" width="306"/>
         </div>
         <div class="clear">
         </div>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Inspiring: The show was inspired by this woman's video, which showed her giving birth in a creek bed and has racked up 20 million views since February
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          However, critics saw the people who may feel compelled to 'try this at home,' as it were, won't have the luxury of a TV crew.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          That means these impressionable souls could be in even greater danger, the position some would say the inspiration for the show was in when she documented for YouTube her own birth in nature.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          YouTube user
          <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=EsNhCWsDVQI" rel="nofollow" style="font-weight:bold;" target="_blank">
           Birthinnature
          </a>
          has just one video associated with her account, but that single offering has racked up an incredible 20 million views since it was posted in February.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          It shows the slow process of a woman giving birth from start to finish, while surrounded by her family, in a creek bed.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          'It has had a profound effect on my mothering and for my children especially,' the mother in the video said of the nature birth.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          The subjects of Born in the Wild who are after that same motherly high have yet to be revealed, but Lehrer says there aren't all that many of them.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          'I truly dont think this is something people would enter into lightly,' he says. 'This is a very specific subset of people doing this.'
         </font>
        </p>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
        <div class="artSplitter">
         <img alt="Dangerous: Critics fear the show will encourage parents to endanger their children but producers say only a small subset of people would ever choose to participate in such a birth" class="blkBorder img-share" height="325" id="i-12e13486aee9b01b" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2014/06/05/article-0-1E7B6EC700000578-769_634x325.jpg" width="634"/>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Dangerous: Critics fear the show will encourage parents to endanger their children but producers say only a small subset of people would ever choose to participate in such a birth
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
        </p>

       <script async="" src="//cdn.taboola.com/libtrc/dailymail-us/loader.js">
       </script>
       <script type="text/javascript">
        DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '&lt;div id="' + id + '"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
            $(node).after(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n});
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=news&amp;pageSize=10',
            total: 19.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
       </script>

               <img alt="The Cascadia Earthquake.

Cascadia_earthquake_sources.png  
Cascadia subduction zone
From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia

The area of the Cascadia subduction zone.
Coordinates: 45N 124W The Cascadia subduction zone (also referred to as the Cascadia fault) is a convergent plate boundary that stretches from northern Vancouver Island to northern California. It is a very long sloping subduction zone fault that separates the Juan de Fuca and North America plates.

The denser oceanic plate is subducting beneath the less dense continental plate offshore of British Columbia, Washington and Oregon. The North American Plate moves in a general southwest direction, overriding the oceanic plate. The Cascadia Subduction Zone is where the two plates meet.

Tectonic processes active in the Cascadia subduction zone region include accretion, subduction, deep earthquakes, and active volcanism that has included such notable eruptions as Mount Mazama (Crater Lake) about 7,500 years ago, Mount Meager a" height="43" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2015/07/14/19/2A874F1000000578-0-image-m-75_1436899600068.jpg" width="45"/>
